{\ttfamily \#include $<$triangle\+\_\+mesh.\+h$>$}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{class}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{ELEMENT}}$>$\newline
class oomph\+::\+Triangle\+Mesh$<$ ELEMENT $>$}
Triangle mesh build with the help of the scaffold mesh coming from the triangle mesh generator Triangle. \href{http://www.cs.cmu.edu/~quake/triangle.html}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+cs.\+cmu.\+edu/\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}quake/triangle.\+html}}.

Re-\/assign the boundary segments initial zeta (arclength) for those internal boundaries that were splited during the distribution process. Those boundaries that have one face element at each side of the boundary. Here we create the segments only with the nonhalo elements, therefore the boundary coordinates need to be re-\/assigned to be passed to the new meshes.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{class}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{ELEMENT}} $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TriangleMesh}{oomph\+::\+Triangle\+Mesh}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{ELEMENT}} $>$\+::select\+\_\+boundary\+\_\+face\+\_\+elements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{Vector}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{Finite\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ \&}]{face\+\_\+ele\+\_\+pt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{unsigned}} \&}]{b,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{bool}} \&}]{is\+\_\+internal\+\_\+boundary,  }\item[{std\+::map$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{Finite\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1TetgenMesh}{Finite\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ \&}]{face\+\_\+to\+\_\+bulk\+\_\+element\+\_\+pt }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Select face element from boundary using the criteria to decide which of the two face elements should be used on internal boundaries. 

===================================================================== Select face elements from a given boundary. In case the we are dealing with an internal boundary we use a set of criterias to decide which of the two face elements should be used on represent the internal boundary. We return the face elements, halo or haloed on this processor that form the boundary. The caller method should be in charge of selecting nonhalo elements and deleting the face\hypertarget{classoomph_1_1TriangleMesh_autotoc_md1}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{elements created by this method}{elements created by this method}}\label{classoomph_1_1TriangleMesh_autotoc_md1}

Delete those outside/inside the outer polygons (this is required since Triangle can not deal with vertices that define holes outside the new outer polygons of the domain)
